        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





There is a heap buffer overflow vulnerability in the Vulkan backend that could be triggered in Swiftshader.



<span class="line"><!---->There is a heap buffer overflow vulnerability in the Vulkan backend that could be triggered in Swiftshader.<!----></span>



<br>





I think it seems that ImageHelper::SubresourceUpdate::isUpdateToLayers is the cause.



<span class="line"><!---->I think it seems that ImageHelper::SubresourceUpdate::isUpdateToLayers is the cause.<!----></span>



<br>





This vulnerability started in commit 



<span class="line"><!---->This vulnerability started in commit <!----></span>





56330564295ef041b63c82283142eed8b98e2087



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/56330564295ef041b63c82283142eed8b98e2087"><!---->56330564295ef041b63c82283142eed8b98e2087<!----></a>





.



<span class="line"><!---->.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





-------------------------



<b class="line"><!---->-------------------------<!----></b>





--------------------------------------------------------------



<span class="line"><!---->--------------------------------------------------------------<!----></span>



<br>





-- bool ImageHelper::SubresourceUpdate::isUpdateToLayer(uint32_t layerIndex) const



<span class="line"><!---->-- bool ImageHelper::SubresourceUpdate::isUpdateToLayer(uint32_t layerIndex) const<!----></span>



<br>





++ bool ImageHelper::SubresourceUpdate::isUpdateToLayers(uint32_t layerIndex, uint32_t layerCount) const



<span class="line"><!---->++ bool ImageHelper::SubresourceUpdate::isUpdateToLayers(uint32_t layerIndex, uint32_t layerCount) const<!----></span>



<br>





{



<span class="line"><!---->{<!----></span>



<br>





    uint32_t updateBaseLayer, updateLayerCount;



<span class="line"><!---->    uint32_t updateBaseLayer, updateLayerCount;<!----></span>



<br>





    getDestSubresource(gl::ImageIndex::kEntireLevel, &updateBaseLayer, &updateLayerCount);



<span class="line"><!---->    getDestSubresource(gl::ImageIndex::kEntireLevel, &amp;updateBaseLayer, &amp;updateLayerCount);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





--    return updateBaseLayer == layerIndex;



<span class="line"><!---->--    return updateBaseLayer == layerIndex;<!----></span>



<br>





++    return updateBaseLayer == layerIndex && (updateLayerCount == layerCount || updateLayerCount == VK_REMAINING_ARRAY_LAYERS);



<span class="line"><!---->++    return updateBaseLayer == layerIndex &amp;&amp; (updateLayerCount == layerCount || updateLayerCount == VK_REMAINING_ARRAY_LAYERS);<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





-------------------------



<b class="line"><!---->-------------------------<!----></b>





--------------------------------------------------------------



<span class="line"><!---->--------------------------------------------------------------<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When redefining the texture, the code before the commit above removes levelUpdates as long as the layerIndex is the same.



<span class="line"><!---->When redefining the texture, the code before the commit above removes levelUpdates as long as the layerIndex is the same.<!----></span>



<br>





However, since the condition "updateLayerCount == layerCount" has been added, levelUpdates will not be removed if the depth(layerCount) in texImage3D is different.



<span class="line"><!---->However, since the condition "updateLayerCount == layerCount" has been added, levelUpdates will not be removed if the depth(layerCount) in texImage3D is different.<!----></span>



<br>





This will lead to incorrect behavior. Also this can lead to heap buffer overflow.



<span class="line"><!---->This will lead to incorrect behavior. Also this can lead to heap buffer overflow.<!----></span>



<br>





(In addition to this vulnerability, if levelUpdates is not properly removed for any reason, memory corruption may occur in vk::Image::copy, copy... functions.)



<span class="line"><!---->(In addition to this vulnerability, if levelUpdates is not properly removed for any reason, memory corruption may occur in vk::Image::copy, copy... functions.)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>



<br>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: master (and tested on 97.0.4692.99 (Official Build) (64-bit) Stable)



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: master (and tested on 97.0.4692.99 (Official Build) (64-bit) Stable)<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Windows 10 x64



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Windows 10 x64<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>



<br>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





Run the attached poc.html (with --disable-gpu)



<span class="line"><!---->Run the attached poc.html (with --disable-gpu)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>



<br>



<br>



<br>





FOR CRASHES, PLEASE INCLUDE THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL INFORMATION



<b class="line"><!---->FOR CRASHES, PLEASE INCLUDE THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL INFORMATION<!----></b>



<br>





Type of crash: GPU Process



<span class="line"><!---->Type of crash: GPU Process<!----></span>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->Crash State:<!----></span>

Vulkan: Fix texture array level redefinition



<span class="line"><!---->Vulkan: Fix texture array level redefinition<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When a level of a texture is redefined, all staged updates to that level



<span class="line"><!---->When a level of a texture is redefined, all staged updates to that level<!----></span>



<br>





should be removed, not the ones specific to the new layers.  The bug



<span class="line"><!---->should be removed, not the ones specific to the new layers.  The bug<!----></span>



<br>





fixed was that if the texture was redefined to have its number of layers



<span class="line"><!---->fixed was that if the texture was redefined to have its number of layers<!----></span>



<br>





changed, the staged higher-layer-count update to the image was not



<span class="line"><!---->changed, the staged higher-layer-count update to the image was not<!----></span>



<br>





removed.



<span class="line"><!---->removed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. M99: Vulkan: Fix texture array level redefinition



<span class="line"><!---->M99: Vulkan: Fix texture array level redefinition<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When a level of a texture is redefined, all staged updates to that level



<span class="line"><!---->When a level of a texture is redefined, all staged updates to that level<!----></span>



<br>





should be removed, not the ones specific to the new layers.  The bug



<span class="line"><!---->should be removed, not the ones specific to the new layers.  The bug<!----></span>



<br>





fixed was that if the texture was redefined to have its number of layers



<span class="line"><!---->fixed was that if the texture was redefined to have its number of layers<!----></span>



<br>





changed, the staged higher-layer-count update to the image was not



<span class="line"><!---->changed, the staged higher-layer-count update to the image was not<!----></span>



<br>





removed.



<span class="line"><!---->removed.<!----></span>

[M96-LTS] Vulkan: Fix texture array level redefinition



<span class="line"><!---->[M96-LTS] Vulkan: Fix texture array level redefinition<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When a level of a texture is redefined, all staged updates to that level



<span class="line"><!---->When a level of a texture is redefined, all staged updates to that level<!----></span>



<br>





should be removed, not the ones specific to the new layers.  The bug



<span class="line"><!---->should be removed, not the ones specific to the new layers.  The bug<!----></span>



<br>





fixed was that if the texture was redefined to have its number of layers



<span class="line"><!---->fixed was that if the texture was redefined to have its number of layers<!----></span>



<br>





changed, the staged higher-layer-count update to the image was not



<span class="line"><!---->changed, the staged higher-layer-count update to the image was not<!----></span>



<br>





removed.



<span class="line"><!---->removed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

Vulkan: Fix texture array level redefinition



<span class="line"><!---->Vulkan: Fix texture array level redefinition<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When a level of a texture is redefined, all staged updates to that level



<span class="line"><!---->When a level of a texture is redefined, all staged updates to that level<!----></span>



<br>





should be removed, not the ones specific to the new layers.  The bug



<span class="line"><!---->should be removed, not the ones specific to the new layers.  The bug<!----></span>



<br>





fixed was that if the texture was redefined to have its number of layers



<span class="line"><!---->fixed was that if the texture was redefined to have its number of layers<!----></span>



<br>





changed, the staged higher-layer-count update to the image was not



<span class="line"><!---->changed, the staged higher-layer-count update to the image was not<!----></span>



<br>





removed.



<span class="line"><!---->removed.<!----></span>



<br>

           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
